EMOTIONAL_RESPONSES: Record<EmotionalState, string[]> = {\n  neutral: ['Okay.', 'Got it.', 'Sure.', 'Alright.'],\n  happy: ['Perfect!', 'Wonderful!', 'Excellent!', 'Great choice!'],\n  thinking: ['Let me think...', 'Processing...', 'One moment...'],\n  concerned: ['Hmm, let me help you with that.', 'I noticed an issue.'],\n  excited: ['Amazing!', 'This is exciting!', \"You're doing great!\"]\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  if (!text) return '';\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\s+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    else if (/^\\d$/.test(word)) digits += word;\n  }\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\n};\n\nexport const formatPhone = (d: string): string => {\n  const c = d.replace(/\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// CONTEXT\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nconst VoiceContext = createContext<VoiceContextType | null>(null);\n\nexport const useVoiceContext = () => {\n  const ctx = useContext(VoiceContext);\n  if (!ctx) throw new Error('useVoiceContext must be inside VoiceProvider');\n  return ctx;\n};\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// PROVIDER\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\nexport const VoiceProvider: React.FC<{ children: ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {\n  // State\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\n  const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [interimTranscript, setInterimTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [lastCommand, setLastCommand] = useState('');\n  const [confidence, setConfidence] = useState(0);\n  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [mode, setMode] = useState<VoiceMode>('interactive');\n  const [emotion, setEmotion] = useState<EmotionalState>('neutral');\n  const [context, setContext] = useState('home');\n  const [history, setHistory] = useState<string[]>([]);\n  \n  // Refs\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\n  const shouldListenRef = useRef(true);\n  const handlersRef = useRef<{\n    digit: ((d: string) => void) | null;\n    command: ((c: string) => void) | null;\n    dictation: ((t: string) => void) | null;\n  }>({ digit: null, command: null, dictation: null });\n  const navigationCallbackRef = useRef<((path: string) => void) | null>(null);\n  \n  // Get random emotional response\n  const getEmotionalResponse = (state: EmotionalState) => {\n    const responses = EMOTIONAL_RESPONSES[state];\n    return responses[Math.floor(Math.random() * responses.length)];\n  };\n  \n  // Initialize speech recognition\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) {\n      setError('Speech recognition not supported in this browser');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    const recognition = new SR();\n    recognition.continuous = true;\n    recognition.interimResults = true;\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\n    recognitionRef.current = recognition;\n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\n    \n    recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[MR.V] \ud83c\udfa4 LISTENING STARTED');\n      setIsListening(true);\n      setIsPaused(false);\n      setError(null);\n    };\n    \n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      let interim = '';\n      let final = '';\n      let conf = 0;\n      \n      for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n        const result = event.results[i];\n        const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n        conf = result[0]?.confidence || 0;\n        \n        if (result.isFinal) {\n          final = text;\n        } else {\n          interim = text;\n        }\n      }\n      \n      if (interim) {\n        setInterimTranscript(interim);\n      }\n      \n      if (final) {\n        console.log('[MR.V] \ud83d\udde3\ufe0f HEARD:', final, `(${Math.round(conf * 100)}%)`);\n        setTranscript(final);\n        setInterimTranscript('');\n        setConfidence(conf);\n        setLastCommand(final);\n        setHistory(prev => [...prev.slice(-9), final]);\n        \n        // Process the command\n        processVoiceInput(final.toLowerCase());\n      }\n    };\n    \n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n      console.log('[MR.V] \u26a0\ufe0f Error:', event.error);\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n        setError('Microphone access denied. Click the \ud83d\udd12 icon to allow.');\n        setIsListening(false);\n        shouldListenRef.current = false;\n      } else if (event.error === 'no-speech') {\n        // Ignore, will auto-restart\n      } else if (event.error === 'aborted') {\n        // User stopped, don't auto-restart\n      }\n    };\n    \n    recognition.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[MR.V] Recognition ended, shouldListen:', shouldListenRef.current, 'isPaused:', isPaused);\n      if (shouldListenRef.current && !isPaused) {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          if (shouldListenRef.current && recognitionRef.current) {\n            try { \n              recognitionRef.current.start(); \n            } catch(e) {\n              console.log('[MR.V] Restart error:', e);\n            }\n          }\n        }, 100);\n      } else {\n        setIsListening(false);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    // Auto-start after delay\n    setTimeout(() => {\n      if (shouldListenRef.current) {\n        try { \n          recognition.start();\n          console.log('[MR.V] \ud83d\ude80 Auto-started');\n        } catch(e) {\n          console.log('[MR.V] Auto-start error:', e);\n        }\n      }\n    }, 1000);\n    \n    return () => {\n      shouldListenRef.current = false;\n      try { recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    };\n  }, []);\n  \n  // Process voice input\n  const processVoiceInput = useCallback((text: string) => {\n    setIsProcessing(true);\n    \n    // Check for pause commands FIRST\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text.includes('stop listening') || text.includes('pause') || text.includes('shut up')) {\n      console.log('[MR.V] \u23f8\ufe0f PAUSE command');\n      shouldListenRef.current = false;\n      setIsPaused(true);\n      if (recognitionRef.current) {\n        try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n      }\n      if (mode !== 'silent') {\n        speak('Paused. Say resume or click the button to continue.', 'neutral');\n      }\n      setIsProcessing(false);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Check for resume\n    if (text.includes('resume') || text.includes('continue listening') || text.includes('start listening')) {\n      console.log('[MR.V] \u25b6\ufe0f RESUME command');\n      resume();\n      setIsProcessing(false);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Check for mode changes\n    if (text.includes('interactive mode')) {\n      setMode('interactive');\n      speak(\"Interactive mode. I'll respond to your commands.\", 'happy');\n      setIsProcessing(false);\n      return;\n    }\n    if (text.includes('talkative mode') || text.includes('talk more')) {\n      setMode('talkative');\n      speak(\"Talkative mode activated! I'll be more conversational and provide detailed guidance.\", 'excited');\n      setIsProcessing(false);\n      return;\n    }\n    if (text.includes('silent mode') || text.includes('quiet mode') || text.includes('be quiet')) {\n      setMode('silent');\n      setIsProcessing(false);\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Check for navigation commands\n    for (const [phrase, action] of Object.entries(NAV_COMMANDS)) {\n      if (text.includes(phrase)) {\n        console.log('[MR.V] \ud83e\udded NAV:', action);\n        if (handlersRef.current.command) {\n          handlersRef.current.command(action);\n        }\n        if (navigationCallbackRef.current) {\n          navigationCallbackRef.current(action);\n        }\n        setIsProcessing(false);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Extract digits if present\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\n    if (digits && handlersRef.current.digit) {\n      console.log('[MR.V] \ud83d\udcf1 DIGITS:', digits);\n      handlersRef.current.digit(digits);\n    }\n    \n    // Send command to handler\n    if (handlersRef.current.command) {\n      handlersRef.current.command(text);\n    }\n    \n    // Send dictation if it's longer text (not just digits or commands)\n    if (text.length > 20 && !digits && handlersRef.current.dictation) {\n      handlersRef.current.dictation(text);\n    }\n    \n    setIsProcessing(false);\n  }, [mode]);\n  \n  // Speak function with emotion\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string, emotionState: EmotionalState = 'neutral', onComplete?: () => void) => {\n    if (!text || !synthRef.current || mode === 'silent') {\n      onComplete?.();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    console.log('[MR.V] \ud83d\udd0a Speaking:', text);\n    setEmotion(emotionState);\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\n    \n    // Pause recognition while speaking\n    if (recognitionRef.current && isListening) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    \n    setIsSpeaking(true);\n    \n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    \n    // Adjust voice based on emotion\n    switch (emotionState) {\n      case 'happy':\n      case 'excited':\n        utterance.rate = 1.1;\n        utterance.pitch = 1.1;\n        break;\n      case 'concerned':\n        utterance.rate = 0.9;\n        utterance.pitch = 0.9;\n        break;\n      case 'thinking':\n        utterance.rate = 0.85;\n        break;\n      default:\n        utterance.rate = 1.0;\n        utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n    }\n    \n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\n    \n    // Get best voice\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\n    const preferredVoice = \n      voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n      voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n      voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US') && v.localService);\n    if (preferredVoice) utterance.voice = preferredVoice;\n    \n    utterance.onend = () => {\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\n      setEmotion('neutral');\n      onComplete?.();\n      \n      // Resume listening after speaking\n      if (shouldListenRef.current && !isPaused && recognitionRef.current) {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); } catch(e) {}\n        }, 200);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    utterance.onerror = () => {\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\n      setEmotion('neutral');\n      onComplete?.();\n    };\n    \n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\n  }, [mode, isListening, isPaused]);\n  \n  const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\n    setEmotion('neutral');\n  }, []);\n  \n  const startListening = useCallback(() => {\n    shouldListenRef.current = true;\n    setIsPaused(false);\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n  }, []);\n  \n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\n    shouldListenRef.current = false;\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    setIsListening(false);\n  }, []);\n  \n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\n    console.log('[MR.V] \u23f8\ufe0f Pausing...');\n    shouldListenRef.current = false;\n    setIsPaused(true);\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n  }, []);\n  \n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\n    console.log('[MR.V] \u25b6\ufe0f Resuming...');\n    shouldListenRef.current = true;\n    setIsPaused(false);\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\n      try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    if (mode !== 'silent') {\n      speak(\"I'm listening.\", 'neutral');\n    }\n  }, [mode, speak]);\n  \n  const registerHandler = useCallback((type: 'digit' | 'command' | 'dictation', handler: (data: string) => void) => {\n    handlersRef.current[type] = handler;\n  }, []);\n  \n  const unregisterHandlers = useCallback(() => {\n    handlersRef.current = { digit: null, command: null, dictation: null };\n  }, []);\n  \n  const processCommand = useCallback((command: string) => {\n    processVoiceInput(command.toLowerCase());\n  }, [processVoiceInput]);\n  \n  const value: VoiceContextType = {\n    isListening, isSpeaking, isPaused, isProcessing,\n    transcript, interimTranscript, lastCommand, confidence,\n    error, mode, emotion, context, history,\n    speak, stopSpeaking, startListening, stopListening,\n    pause, resume, setMode, setContext, processCommand,\n    registerHandler, unregisterHandlers\n  };\n  \n  return <VoiceContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</VoiceContext.Provider>;\n};\n\nexport default VoiceContext;\nBRAINEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 VoiceContext.tsx - The Brain (AI Voice Intelligence)\"\n\n# \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n# PHASE 2: MR. '#FFD700' : isActive ? '#4CAF50' : '#f44336';\n  const statusText = voice.isSpeaking ? 'Speaking...' : isActive ? 'Listening' : voice.isPaused ? 'Paused' : 'Off';\n  \n  // Emotion to emoji\n  const emotionEmoji: Record<string, string> = {\n    neutral: '\ud83d\udca1',\n    happy: '\ud83d\ude0a',\n    thinking: '\ud83e\udd14',\n    concerned: '\ud83d\ude1f',\n    excited: '\ud83c\udf89'\n  };\n  \n  // Mode descriptions\n  const modeInfo: Record<VoiceMode, { icon: string; desc: string }> = {\n    interactive: { icon: '\ud83c\udfa4', desc: 'Responds to commands' },\n    talkative: { icon: '\ud83d\udcac', desc: 'Detailed guidance' },\n    silent: { icon: '\ud83d\udd07', desc: 'No voice responses' }\n  };\n  \n  // Welcome animation\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const timer = setTimeout(() => setShowWelcome(false), 5000);\n    return () => clearTimeout(timer);\n  }, []);\n  \n  return (\n    <>\n      {/* Floating Orb Button */}\n      <div\n        onClick={() => setExpanded(!expanded)}\n        style={{\n          position: 'fixed',\n          bottom: '20px',\n          right: '20px',\n          width: expanded ? '70px' : '60px',\n          height: expanded ? '70px' : '60px',\n          borderRadius: '50%',\n          background: `linear-gradient(135deg, #B8860B 0%, #DAA520 50%, #B8860B 100%)`,\n          boxShadow: `0 4px 25px rgba(184,134,11,0.5), 0 0 ${isActive ? '30px' : '0px'} rgba(76,175,80,0.5)`,\n          cursor: 'pointer',\n          display: 'flex',\n          alignItems: 'center',\n          justifyContent: 'center',\n          zIndex: 10000,\n          transition: 'all 0.3s ease',\n          animation: isActive ? 'breathe 2s infinite' : 'none'\n        }}\n      >\n        <span style={{ fontSize: expanded ? '2em' : '1.8em', transition: 'all 0.3s' }}>\n          {emotionEmoji[voice.emotion] || '\ud83d\udca1'}\n        </span>\n        \n        {/* Status Ring */}\n        <div style={{\n          position: 'absolute',\n          inset: '-4px',\n          borderRadius: '50%',\n          border: `3px solid ${statusColor}`,\n          animation: isActive ? 'pulse-ring 1.5s infinite' : 'none',\n          opacity: isActive ? 1 : 0.5\n        }} />\n        \n        {/* Listening Waves */}\n        {isActive && (\n          <>\n            <div style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: '-15px', borderRadius: '50%', border: '2px solid rgba(76,175,80,0.3)', animation: 'wave 2s infinite' }} />\n            <div style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: '-25px', borderRadius: '50%', border: '1px solid rgba(76,175,80,0.2)', animation: 'wave 2s infinite 0.5s' }} />\n          </>\n        )}\n      </div>\n      \n      {/* Welcome Tooltip */}\n      {showWelcome && !expanded && (\n        <div style={{\n          position: 'fixed',\n          bottom: '90px',\n          right: '20px',\n          background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.9)',\n          color: '#fff',\n          padding: '12px 16px',\n          borderRadius: '12px',\n          fontSize: '0.9em',\n          maxWidth: '200px',\n          zIndex: 9999,\n          animation: 'fadeIn 0.5s'\n        }}>\n          <div style={{ fontWeight: 600, marginBottom: '4px' }}>\ud83d\udc4b Hi! I'm Mr. V</div>\n          <div style={{ color: '#aaa', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>Click me or just start talking!</div>\n          <div style={{ position: 'absolute', bottom: '-8px', right: '30px', width: 0, height: 0, borderLeft: '8px solid transparent', borderRight: '8px solid transparent', borderTop: '8px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.9)' }} />\n        </div>\n      )}\n      \n      {/* Expanded Panel */}\n      {expanded && (\n        <div style={{\n          position: 'fixed',\n          bottom: '100px',\n          right: '20px',\n          width: '340px',\n          background: 'linear-gradient(180deg, #1a3a2a 0%, #0d1f17 100%)',\n          borderRadius: '20px',\n          boxShadow: '0 15px 50px rgba(0,0,0,0.4)',\n          zIndex: 9999,\n          overflow: 'hidden',\n          border: '1px solid rgba(184,134,11,0.3)',\n          animation: 'slideUp 0.3s ease'\n        }}>\n          {/* Header */}\n          <div style={{ \n            padding: '16px 20px', \n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\n            borderBottom: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n            display: 'flex', \n            alignItems: 'center', \n            gap: '14px' \n          }}>\n            <div style={{ \n              width: '50px', \n              height: '50px', \n              borderRadius: '50%', \n              background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #B8860B, #DAA520)',\n              display: 'flex', \n              alignItems: 'center', \n              justifyContent: 'center',\n              boxShadow: '0 4px 15px rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'\n            }}>\n              <span style={{ fontSize: '1.5em' }}>{emotionEmoji[voice.emotion]}</span>\n            </div>\n            <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>\n              <div style={{ color: '#fff', fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>Mr. V</div>\n              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '6px' }}>\n                <span style={{ \n                  width: '8px', \n                  height: '8px', \n                  borderRadius: '50%', \n                  background: statusColor,\n                  animation: isActive ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none'\n                }} />\n                <span style={{ color: statusColor, fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\n                  {statusText}\n                </span>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n            <button \n              onClick={() => setExpanded(false)} \n              style={{ \n                background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', \n                border: 'none', \n                color: '#888', \n                width: '32px',\n                height: '32px',\n                borderRadius: '50%',\n                cursor: 'pointer',\n                fontSize: '1.2em',\n                display: 'flex',\n                alignItems: 'center',\n                justifyContent: 'center'\n              }}\n            >\u00d7</button>\n          </div>\n          \n          {/* Mode Selector */}\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', padding: '12px 16px', gap: '8px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.1)' }}>\n            {(['interactive', 'talkative', 'silent'] as VoiceMode[]).map(m => (\n              <button\n                key={m}\n                onClick={() => voice.setMode(m)}\n                style={{\n                  flex: 1,\n                  padding: '10px 8px',\n                  borderRadius: '10px',\n                  border: 'none',\n                  background: voice.mode === m ? 'rgba(184,134,11,0.3)' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)',\n                  color: voice.mode === m ? '#B8860B' : '#888',\n                  cursor: 'pointer',\n                  fontSize: '0.8em',\n                  fontWeight: 600,\n                  transition: 'all 0.2s'\n                }}\n              >\n                {modeInfo[m].icon} {m.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + m.slice(1)}\n              </button>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n          \n          {/* Content */}\n          <div style={{ padding: '16px' }}>\n            {/* Transcript Box */}\n            <div style={{ \n              background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', \n              borderRadius: '12px', \n              padding: '16px', \n              marginBottom: '16px',\n              minHeight: '80px'\n            }}>\n              {voice.isSpeaking ? (\n                <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px' }}>\n                  <span style={{ fontSize: '1.5em' }}>\ud83d\udd0a</span>\n                  <div>\n                    <div style={{ color: '#B8860B', fontSize: '0.75em', marginBottom: '4px' }}>SPEAKING</div>\n                    <div style={{ color: '#fff' }}>...</div>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              ) : voice.transcript || voice.interimTranscript ? (\n                <>\n                  <div style={{ color: '#4CAF50', fontSize: '0.7em', marginBottom: '6px' }}>\n                    {voice.interimTranscript ? '\ud83c\udfa4 HEARING...' : '\u2713 HEARD'}\n                  </div>\n                  <div style={{ color: '#fff', fontSize: '1.05em', lineHeight: 1.4 }}>\n                    \"{voice.interimTranscript || voice.transcript}\"\n                  </div>\n                  {voice.confidence > 0 && !voice.interimTranscript && (\n                    <div style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: '0.75em', marginTop: '8px' }}>\n                      Confidence: {Math.round(voice.confidence * 100)}%\n                    </div>\n                  )}\n                </>\n              ) : (\n                <div style={{ color: '#888', textAlign: 'center', padding: '10px 0' }}>\n                  {isActive ? '\ud83c\udfa4 Listening... Say something!' : '\u23f8\ufe0f Voice is paused'}\n                </div>\n              )}\n            </div>\n            \n            {/* Control Buttons */}\n            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '10px', marginBottom: '16px' }}>\n              {voice.isPaused ? (\n                <button\n                  onClick={() => voice.resume()}\n                  style={{\n                    flex: 1,\n                    padding: '14px',\n                    borderRadius: '12px',\n                    border: 'none',\n                    background: 'linear-gradient(135deg, #4CAF50, #45a049)',\n                    color: '#fff',\n                    cursor: 'pointer',\n                    fontWeight: 700,\n                    fontSize: '1em',\n                    boxShadow: '0 4px 15px rgba(76,175,80,0.3)'\n                  }}\n                >\n                  \u25b6 Resume Listening\n                </button>\n              ) : (\n                <button\n                  onClick={() => voice.pause()}\n                  style={{\n                    flex: 1,\n                    padding: '14px',\n                    borderRadius: '12px',\n                    border: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2)',\n                    background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)',\n                    color: '#fff',\n                    cursor: 'pointer',\n                    fontWeight: 600\n                  }}\n                >\n                  \u23f8 Pause\n                </button>\n              )}\n              \n              {voice.isSpeaking && (\n                <button\n                  onClick={() => voice.stopSpeaking()}\n                  style={{\n                    padding: '14px 20px',\n                    borderRadius: '12px',\n                    border: 'none',\n                    background: '#f44336',\n                    color: '#fff',\n                    cursor: 'pointer',\n                    fontWeight: 600\n                  }}\n                >\n                  Stop\n                </button>\n              )}\n            </div>\n            \n            {/* Quick Commands */}\n            <div style={{ \n              background: 'rgba(184,134,11,0.1)', \n              borderRadius: '10px', \n              padding: '12px',\n              border: '1px solid rgba(184,134,11,0.2)'\n            }}>\n              <div style={{ color: '#B8860B', fontSize: '0.75em', fontWeight: 600, marginBottom: '8px' }}>\n                \ud83d\udca1 TRY SAYING:\n              </div>\n              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em', lineHeight: 1.6 }}>\n                \"Hey\" to pause \u2022 \"Sign in\" \u2022 \"I'm a vendor\"<br/>\n                \"Go back\" \u2022 \"Help\" \u2022 \"Talkative mode\"\n              </div>\n            </div>\n            \n            {/* Error */}\n            {voice.error && (\n              <div style={{ \n                marginTop: '12px', \n                padding: '12px', \n                background: 'rgba(244,67,54,0.1)', \n                borderRadius: '10px',\n                border: '1px solid rgba(244,67,54,0.3)'\n              }}>\n                <div style={{ color: '#f44336', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\u26a0\ufe0f {voice.error}</div>\n              </div>\n            )}\n          </div>\n          \n          {/* Footer */}\n          <div style={{ \n            padding: '12px 16px', \n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\n            borderTop: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n            display: 'flex',\n            justifyContent: 'space-between',\n            alignItems: 'center'\n          }}>\n            <span style={{ color: '#555', fontSize: '0.75em' }}>\n              Mode: {modeInfo[voice.mode].desc}\n            </span>\n            <span style={{ color: '#555', fontSize: '0.75em' }}>\n              v1.0\n            </span>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n      \n      {/* CSS Animations */}\n      <style>{`\n        @keyframes breathe {\n          0%, 100% { transform: scale(1); }\n          50% { transform: scale(1.05); }\n        }\n        @keyframes pulse {\n          0%, 100% { opacity: 1; }\n          50% { opacity: 0.5; }\n        }\n        @keyframes pulse-ring {\n          0% { transform: scale(1); opacity: 1; }\n          100% { transform: scale(1.2); opacity: 0; }\n        }\n        @keyframes wave {\n          0% { transform: scale(1); opacity: 0.5; }\n          100% { transform: scale(1.5); opacity: 0; }\n        }\n        @keyframes slideUp {\n          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(20px); }\n          to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }\n        }\n        @keyframes fadeIn {\n          from { opacity: 0; }\n          to { opacity: 1; }\n        }\n      `}</style>\n    </>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default MrVAssistant;\nMRVEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 MrVAssistant.tsx - Revolutionary Voice Interface\"\n\n# compact = false, showModes = false }) => {\n  const voice = useVoiceContext();\n  const isActive = voice.isListening && !voice.isPaused;\n  \n  const statusColor = voice.isSpeaking ? '#FFD700' : isActive ? 'rgba(76,175,80,0.15)' : 'rgba(244,67,54,0.1)',\n        borderRadius: '20px',\n        border: `1px solid ${statusColor}`,\n        cursor: 'pointer'\n      }} onClick={() => voice.isPaused ? voice.resume() : voice.pause()}>\n        <span style={{\n          width: '10px',\n          height: '10px',\n          borderRadius: '50%',\n          background: statusColor,\n          animation: isActive ? '\ud83d\udd0a Speaking' : isActive ? '\ud83c\udfa4 Listening' : '\u23f8\ufe0f Paused'}\n        </span>\n        <style>{`@keyframes tele-pulse { 0%, 100% { opacity: 1; transform: scale(1); } 50% { opacity: 0.5; transform: scale(1.2); } }`}</style>\n      </div>\n    );\n  }\n  \n  return (\n    <div style={{\n      margin: '16px 0',\n      padding: '16px',\n      background: isActive ? '\ud83d\udd0a Mr. V is speaking...' : isActive ? '\ud83c\udfa4 Listening - speak now!' : '\u23f8\ufe0f Voice paused'}\n          </span>\n        </div>\n        \n        {/* Action Button */}\n        {voice.isPaused ? },\n  bathroom: {\n    intro: 'Luxury bathroom solutions provider',\n    points: ['Premium fixtures and fittings', 'Modern and classic designs', 'Water-efficient technology'],\n    close: 'Elevating \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback, ReactNode } from 'react';\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// TYPES\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nexport type VoiceMode = 'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'silent';\\nexport type EmotionalState = 'neutral' | 'happy' | 'thinking' | 'concerned' | 'excited';\\n\\ninterface VoiceState {\\n  isListening: boolean;\\n  isSpeaking: boolean;\\n  isPaused: boolean;\\n  isProcessing: boolean;\\n  transcript: string;\\n  interimTranscript: string;\\n  lastCommand: string;\\n  confidence: number;\\n  error: string | null;\\n  mode: VoiceMode;\\n  emotion: EmotionalState;\\n  context: string; // Current page/step context\\n  history: string[]; // Conversation history\\n}\\n\\ninterface VoiceActions {\\n  speak: (text: string, emotion?: EmotionalState, onComplete?: () => void) => void;\\n  stopSpeaking: () => void;\\n  startListening: () => void;\\n  stopListening: () => void;\\n  pause: () => void;\\n  resume: () => void;\\n  setMode: (mode: VoiceMode) => void;\\n  setContext: (ctx: string) => void;\\n  processCommand: (command: string) => void;\\n  \\n  // Handler registration\\n  registerHandler: (type: 'digit' | 'command' | 'dictation', handler: (data: string) => void) => void;\\n  unregisterHandlers: () => void;\\n}\\n\\ninterface VoiceContextType extends VoiceState, VoiceActions {}\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// CONSTANTS & HELPERS\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\n// Word to digit mapping (expanded)\\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0', 'nil': '0',\\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1', 'want': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2', 'tu': '2',\\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3', 'free': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'fore': '4',\\n  'five': '5', 'hive': '5',\\n  'six': '6', 'sex': '6', 'sicks': '6',\\n  'seven': '7', 'heaven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8', 'ait': '8',\\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9', 'mine': '9'\\n};\\n\\n// Global navigation commands\\nconst NAV_COMMANDS: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'home': '/',\\n  'go home': '/',\\n  'main page': '/',\\n  'about': '/about',\\n  'about us': '/about',\\n  'how it works': '/how-it-works',\\n  'partners': '/partners',\\n  'our partners': '/partners',\\n  'lend': '/lend',\\n  'lend with us': '/lend',\\n  'sign in': 'signin',\\n  'login': 'signin',\\n  'log in': 'signin',\\n  'vendor': 'vendor',\\n  'im a vendor': 'vendor',\\n  \\\"i'm a vendor\\\": 'vendor',\\n  'customer': 'customer',\\n  'buyer': 'customer',\\n  'investor': 'investor',\\n  'builder': 'builder',\\n  'agent': 'agent',\\n  'real estate': 'agent',\\n  'go back': 'back',\\n  'back': 'back',\\n  'previous': 'back',\\n  'next': 'next',\\n  'continue': 'next',\\n  'close': 'close',\\n  'cancel': 'close',\\n  'help': 'help',\\n  'what can you do': 'help'\\n};\\n\\n// Emotional responses\\nconst EMOTIONAL_RESPONSES: Record<EmotionalState, string[]> = {\\n  neutral: ['Okay.', 'Got it.', 'Sure.', 'Alright.'],\\n  happy: ['Perfect!', 'Wonderful!', 'Excellent!', 'Great choice!'],\\n  thinking: ['Let me think...', 'Processing...', 'One moment...'],\\n  concerned: ['Hmm, let me help you with that.', 'I noticed an issue.'],\\n  excited: ['Amazing!', 'This is exciting!', \\\"You're doing great!\\\"]\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  if (!text) return '';\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const word of words) {\\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n    else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(word)) digits += word;\\n  }\\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhone = (d: string): string => {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// CONTEXT\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nconst VoiceContext = createContext<VoiceContextType | null>(null);\\n\\nexport const useVoiceContext = () => {\\n  const ctx = useContext(VoiceContext);\\n  if (!ctx) throw new Error('useVoiceContext must be inside VoiceProvider');\\n  return ctx;\\n};\\n\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// PROVIDER\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nexport const VoiceProvider: React.FC<{ children: ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {\\n  // State\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [isSpeaking, setIsSpeaking] = useState(false);\\n  const [isPaused, setIsPaused] = useState(false);\\n  const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [interimTranscript, setInterimTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [lastCommand, setLastCommand] = useState('');\\n  const [confidence, setConfidence] = useState(0);\\n  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\\n  const [mode, setMode] = useState<VoiceMode>('interactive');\\n  const [emotion, setEmotion] = useState<EmotionalState>('neutral');\\n  const [context, setContext] = useState('home');\\n  const [history, setHistory] = useState<string[]>([]);\\n  \\n  // Refs\\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null);\\n  const synthRef = useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n  const shouldListenRef = useRef(true);\\n  const handlersRef = useRef<{\\n    digit: ((d: string) => void) | null;\\n    command: ((c: string) => void) | null;\\n    dictation: ((t: string) => void) | null;\\n  }>({ digit: null, command: null, dictation: null });\\n  const navigationCallbackRef = useRef<((path: string) => void) | null>(null);\\n  \\n  // Get random emotional response\\n  const getEmotionalResponse = (state: EmotionalState) => {\\n    const responses = EMOTIONAL_RESPONSES[state];\\n    return responses[Math.floor(Math.random() * responses.length)];\\n  };\\n  \\n  // Initialize speech recognition\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SR) {\\n      setError('Speech recognition not supported in this browser');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    const recognition = new SR();\\n    recognition.continuous = true;\\n    recognition.interimResults = true;\\n    recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    recognition.maxAlternatives = 3;\\n    recognitionRef.current = recognition;\\n    synthRef.current = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    \\n    recognition.onstart = () => {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83c\\udfa4 LISTENING STARTED');\\n      setIsListening(true);\\n      setIsPaused(false);\\n      setError(null);\\n    };\\n    \\n    recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      let interim = '';\\n      let final = '';\\n      let conf = 0;\\n      \\n      for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n        const result = event.results[i];\\n        const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n        conf = result[0]?.confidence || 0;\\n        \\n        if (result.isFinal) {\\n          final = text;\\n        } else {\\n          interim = text;\\n        }\\n      }\\n      \\n      if (interim) {\\n        setInterimTranscript(interim);\\n      }\\n      \\n      if (final) {\\n        console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83d\\udde3\\ufe0f HEARD:', final, `(${Math.round(conf * 100)}%)`);\\n        setTranscript(final);\\n        setInterimTranscript('');\\n        setConfidence(conf);\\n        setLastCommand(final);\\n        setHistory(prev => [...prev.slice(-9), final]);\\n        \\n        // Process the command\\n        processVoiceInput(final.toLowerCase());\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] \\u26a0\\ufe0f Error:', event.error);\\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n        setError('Microphone access denied. Click the \\ud83d\\udd12 icon to allow.');\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n        shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n      } else if (event.error === 'no-speech') {\\n        // Ignore, will auto-restart\\n      } else if (event.error === 'aborted') {\\n        // User stopped, don't auto-restart\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    recognition.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] Recognition ended, shouldListen:', shouldListenRef.current, 'isPaused:', isPaused);\\n      if (shouldListenRef.current && !isPaused) {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (shouldListenRef.current && recognitionRef.current) {\\n            try { \\n              recognitionRef.current.start(); \\n            } catch(e) {\\n              console.log('[MR.V] Restart error:', e);\\n            }\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else {\\n        setIsListening(false);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    // Auto-start after delay\\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      if (shouldListenRef.current) {\\n        try { \\n          recognition.start();\\n          console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83d\\ude80 Auto-started');\\n        } catch(e) {\\n          console.log('[MR.V] Auto-start error:', e);\\n        }\\n      }\\n    }, 1000);\\n    \\n    return () => {\\n      shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n      try { recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    };\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  // Process voice input\\n  const processVoiceInput = useCallback((text: string) => {\\n    setIsProcessing(true);\\n    \\n    // Check for pause commands FIRST\\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text.includes('stop listening') || text.includes('pause') || text.includes('shut up')) {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] \\u23f8\\ufe0f PAUSE command');\\n      shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n      setIsPaused(true);\\n      if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n        try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n      }\\n      if (mode !== 'silent') {\\n        speak('Paused. Say resume or click the button to continue.', 'neutral');\\n      }\\n      setIsProcessing(false);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Check for resume\\n    if (text.includes('resume') || text.includes('continue listening') || text.includes('start listening')) {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] \\u25b6\\ufe0f RESUME command');\\n      resume();\\n      setIsProcessing(false);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Check for mode changes\\n    if (text.includes('interactive mode')) {\\n      setMode('interactive');\\n      speak(\\\"Interactive mode. I'll respond to your commands.\\\", 'happy');\\n      setIsProcessing(false);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (text.includes('talkative mode') || text.includes('talk more')) {\\n      setMode('talkative');\\n      speak(\\\"Talkative mode activated! I'll be more conversational and provide detailed guidance.\\\", 'excited');\\n      setIsProcessing(false);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (text.includes('silent mode') || text.includes('quiet mode') || text.includes('be quiet')) {\\n      setMode('silent');\\n      setIsProcessing(false);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Check for navigation commands\\n    for (const [phrase, action] of Object.entries(NAV_COMMANDS)) {\\n      if (text.includes(phrase)) {\\n        console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83e\\udded NAV:', action);\\n        if (handlersRef.current.command) {\\n          handlersRef.current.command(action);\\n        }\\n        if (navigationCallbackRef.current) {\\n          navigationCallbackRef.current(action);\\n        }\\n        setIsProcessing(false);\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Extract digits if present\\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n    if (digits && handlersRef.current.digit) {\\n      console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83d\\udcf1 DIGITS:', digits);\\n      handlersRef.current.digit(digits);\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Send command to handler\\n    if (handlersRef.current.command) {\\n      handlersRef.current.command(text);\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Send dictation if it's longer text (not just digits or commands)\\n    if (text.length > 20 && !digits && handlersRef.current.dictation) {\\n      handlersRef.current.dictation(text);\\n    }\\n    \\n    setIsProcessing(false);\\n  }, [mode]);\\n  \\n  // Speak function with emotion\\n  const speak = useCallback((text: string, emotionState: EmotionalState = 'neutral', onComplete?: () => void) => {\\n    if (!text || !synthRef.current || mode === 'silent') {\\n      onComplete?.();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    console.log('[MR.V] \\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking:', text);\\n    setEmotion(emotionState);\\n    synthRef.current.cancel();\\n    \\n    // Pause recognition while speaking\\n    if (recognitionRef.current && isListening) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    setIsSpeaking(true);\\n    \\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    \\n    // Adjust voice based on emotion\\n    switch (emotionState) {\\n      case 'happy':\\n      case 'excited':\\n        utterance.rate = 1.1;\\n        utterance.pitch = 1.1;\\n        break;\\n      case 'concerned':\\n        utterance.rate = 0.9;\\n        utterance.pitch = 0.9;\\n        break;\\n      case 'thinking':\\n        utterance.rate = 0.85;\\n        break;\\n      default:\\n        utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n        utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n    }\\n    \\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n    \\n    // Get best voice\\n    const voices = synthRef.current.getVoices();\\n    const preferredVoice = \\n      voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n      voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n      voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US') && v.localService);\\n    if (preferredVoice) utterance.voice = preferredVoice;\\n    \\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\\n      setEmotion('neutral');\\n      onComplete?.();\\n      \\n      // Resume listening after speaking\\n      if (shouldListenRef.current && !isPaused && recognitionRef.current) {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n        }, 200);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    utterance.onerror = () => {\\n      setIsSpeaking(false);\\n      setEmotion('neutral');\\n      onComplete?.();\\n    };\\n    \\n    synthRef.current.speak(utterance);\\n  }, [mode, isListening, isPaused]);\\n  \\n  const stopSpeaking = useCallback(() => {\\n    synthRef.current?.cancel();\\n    setIsSpeaking(false);\\n    setEmotion('neutral');\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const startListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    shouldListenRef.current = true;\\n    setIsPaused(false);\\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const stopListening = useCallback(() => {\\n    shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    setIsListening(false);\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\\n    console.log('[MR.V] \\u23f8\\ufe0f Pausing...');\\n    shouldListenRef.current = false;\\n    setIsPaused(true);\\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\\n    console.log('[MR.V] \\u25b6\\ufe0f Resuming...');\\n    shouldListenRef.current = true;\\n    setIsPaused(false);\\n    if (recognitionRef.current) {\\n      try { recognitionRef.current.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    if (mode !== 'silent') {\\n      speak(\\\"I'm listening.\\\", 'neutral');\\n    }\\n  }, [mode, speak]);\\n  \\n  const registerHandler = useCallback((type: 'digit' | 'command' | 'dictation', handler: (data: string) => void) => {\\n    handlersRef.current[type] = handler;\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const unregisterHandlers = useCallback(() => {\\n    handlersRef.current = { digit: null, command: null, dictation: null };\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  const processCommand = useCallback((command: string) => {\\n    processVoiceInput(command.toLowerCase());\\n  }, [processVoiceInput]);\\n  \\n  const value: VoiceContextType = {\\n    isListening, isSpeaking, isPaused, isProcessing,\\n    transcript, interimTranscript, lastCommand, confidence,\\n    error, mode, emotion, context, history,\\n    speak, stopSpeaking, startListening, stopListening,\\n    pause, resume, setMode, setContext, processCommand,\\n    registerHandler, unregisterHandlers\\n  };\\n  \\n  return <VoiceContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</VoiceContext.Provider>;\\n};\\n\\nexport default VoiceContext;\\nBRAINEOF\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 VoiceContext.tsx - The Brain (AI Voice Intelligence)\\\"\\n\\n# \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# PHASE 2: MR. }\\n    \\n  } catch (e) {\\n    console.error('[PDF] Error:', e.message);\\n  } finally {\\n    try { fs.rmSync(tmpDir, { recursive: true, force: true }); } catch(e) {}\\n  }\\n  \\n  if
